{"type":"item.started","item":{"id":"item_16","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"python3 - <<'PY'\nimport os,re,pandas as pd,numpy as np\n# load\nprod=pd.read_csv('production_batches.csv')\nassign=pd.read_csv('machine_assignment_log.csv')\nqi=pd.read_csv('quality_inspections.csv')\nproducts=pd.read_csv('products.csv')\n# parse maint\nrows=[]\nfor root,_,files in os.walk('raw_service_reports'):\n  for fn in files:\n    path=os.path.join(root,fn)\n    d={}\n    for line in open(path):\n      if ':' in line:\n        k,v=line.strip().split(':',1); d[k.strip()]=v.strip()\n    rows.append(d|{'report_path':path})\nserv=pd.DataFrame(rows).rename(columns={'DAY':'day','WORK ORDER':'work_order_id','MACHINE':'machine_id','TECHNICIAN':'technician_id','WORK TYPE':'work_type','REPORTED REASON':'reported_reason','STARTED':'started','COMPLETED':'completed','FINAL STATUS':'final_status'})\nserv['day']=serv.day.astype(int)\ndef minofday(s):\n    h,m=map(int,s.split(':')); return h*60+m\nserv['completed_abs']=(serv.day-1)*1440+serv.completed.map(minofday)\nserv['started_abs']=(serv.day-1)*1440+serv.started.map(minofday)\nserv=serv.sort_values(['machine_id','completed_abs']).reset_index(drop=True)\nserv['next_completed_abs']=serv.groupby('machine_id')['completed_abs'].shift(-1).fillna(np.inf)\nserv['next_work_order_id']=serv.groupby('machine_id')['work_order_id'].shift(-1)\nassign['start_abs']=(assign.day-1)*1440+assign.start_time.map(minofday)\nassign['end_abs']=(assign.day-1)*1440+assign.end_time.map(minofday)\n# combine batch\nb=prod.merge(assign[['job_id','start_abs','end_abs','sequence_on_machine']], on='job_id', how='left', validate='one_to_one')\nb=b.merge(qi, on=['batch_id','product_id'], how='left', validate='one_to_one')\nb=b.merge(products[['product_id','quality_rejection_threshold_pct']], on='product_id')\n# link by merge_asof per machine\nb_sorted=b.sort_values(['machine_id','start_abs']).reset_index(drop=True)\n# Need merge_asof by machine sorted by start_abs + machine? pandas requires overall sort by key not group maybe sort key first\nlinked=[]\nfor m,grp in b.groupby('machine_id'):\n    s=serv[serv.machine_id==m].sort_values('completed_abs')\n    g=grp.sort_values('start_abs')\n    l=pd.merge_asof(g, s[['work_order_id','technician_id','machine_id','work_type','reported_reason','completed_abs','next_completed_abs']], left_on='start_abs', right_on='completed_abs', direction='backward', allow_exact_matches=False, suffixes=('','_serv'))\n    # remove if start after next completed? In merge_asof latest before always automatically before next completed; unless none\n    l.loc[~(l.start_abs < l.next_completed_abs), ['work_order_id','technician_id','work_type','reported_reason','completed_abs','next_completed_abs']]=np.nan\n    linked.append(l)\nlinked=pd.concat(linked, ignore_index=True)\nrej=linked[linked.inspection_result=='REJECTED'].copy()\nprint('batches',len(linked),'rejected',len(rej),'linked rejects',rej.work_order_id.notna().sum(),'unlinked rejects',rej.work_order_id.isna().sum())\n# counts by tech naive\nct=rej.dropna(subset=['technician_id']).groupby('technician_id').agg(rejected_batches=('batch_id','nunique'), work_orders=('work_order_id','nunique'), products=('product_id', lambda x: ','.join(sorted(x.unique())))).sort_values('rejected_batches',ascending=False)\nprint('naive tech counts top all threshold')\nprint(ct.head(50).to_string())\nprint('threshold naive')\nprint(ct[(ct.rejected_batches>=3)&(ct.work_orders>=2)].to_string())\n# counts by work order top\nwo=rej.dropna(subset=['work_order_id']).groupby(['technician_id','work_order_id','machine_id','day']).agg(rejs=('batch_id','nunique'), products=('product_id',lambda x: ','.join(sorted(x.unique()))), days=('production_day',lambda x:f'{x.min()}-{x.max()}'), maxpct=('rejected_pct','max')).sort_values('rejs',ascending=False)\nprint('top WOs by rejected')\nprint(wo.head(60).to_string())\n# product-tech counts naive\npt=rej.dropna(subset=['technician_id']).groupby(['product_id','technician_id']).size().unstack(fill_value=0)\nfor tech in ct[(ct.rejected_batches>=3)&(ct.work_orders>=2)].index:\n    print('\\\\nTECH',tech)\n    print(rej[rej.technician_id==tech].sort_values(['work_order_id','production_day','start_abs'])[['batch_id','production_day','machine_id','product_id','rejected_pct','defect_code','work_order_id','work_type','reported_reason']].to_string(index=False))\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}

return h*60+m\n# load/link as before\nprod=pd.read_csv('production_batches.csv'); assign=pd.read_csv('machine_assignment_log.csv'); qi=pd.read_csv('quality_inspections.csv'); products=pd.read_csv('products.csv')\nrows=[]\nfor root,_,files in os.walk('raw_service_reports'):\n for fn in files:\n  path=os.path.join(root,fn); d={}\n  for line in open(path):\n   if ':' in line:\n    k,v=line.strip().split(':',1); d[k.strip()]=v.strip()\n  rows.append(d)\nserv=pd.DataFrame(rows).rename(columns={'DAY':'maint_day','WORK ORDER':'work_order_id','MACHINE':'serv_machine','TECHNICIAN':'technician_id','WORK TYPE':'work_type','REPORTED REASON':'reported_reason','STARTED':'started','COMPLETED':'completed'})\nserv['maint_day']=serv.maint_day.astype(int); {"type":"item.started","item":{"id":"item_34","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/bash -lc \"python3 - <<'PY'\n# Detailed intervals for borderline/confirmed tech work orders\nimport os,pandas as pd,numpy as np\ndef minofday(s): h,m=map(int,s.split(':')); return h*60+m\nprod=pd.read_csv('production_batches.csv'); assign=pd.read_csv('machine_assignment_log.csv'); qi=pd.read_csv('quality_inspections.csv'); products=pd.read_csv('products.csv'); jobs=pd.read_csv('production_jobs.csv')\nrows=[]\nfor root,_,files in os.walk('raw_service_reports'):\n for fn in files:\n  path=os.path.join(root,fn); d={}\n  for line in open(path):\n   if ':' in line:\n    k,v=line.strip().split(':',1); d[k.strip()]=v.strip()\n  rows.append(d)\nserv=pd.DataFrame(rows).rename(columns={'DAY':'maint_day','WORK ORDER':'work_order_id','MACHINE':'serv_machine','TECHNICIAN':'technician_id','WORK TYPE':'work_type','REPORTED REASON':'reported_reason','STARTED':'started','COMPLETED':'completed'})\nserv['maint_day']=serv.maint_day.astype(int);
